--- Commit Message ---
ATM-258 - Allow aliases for Test-Parameters "clientbuildno" and "serverbuildno"

Test-Parameters: clientversion=2.11.51 serverversion=2.10.5 \
                 testlist=runtests

Test-Parameters: clientversion=2.11.51 mdsversion=2.10.5 \
                 ossversion=2.10.5 mgsversion=2.10.5 \
                 testlist=runtests
                 
Test-Parameters: clientversion=2.11 serverversion=2.10 \
                 testlist=runtests

Test-Parameters: clientjob=lustre-b2_10  clientbuildno=0 \
                 serverjob=lustre-master serverbuildno=0 \
                 testlist=runtests fortestonly
